        function addPlaceholders() {
            // Add placeholders to name fields
            var firstNameField = document.getElementById('reg_sr_firstname');
            var lastNameField = document.getElementById('reg_sr_lastname');
            
            if (firstNameField && !firstNameField.getAttribute('placeholder')) {
                firstNameField.setAttribute('placeholder', 'Fornavn *');
                console.log('Added Fornavn placeholder');
            }
            if (lastNameField && !lastNameField.getAttribute('placeholder')) {
                lastNameField.setAttribute('placeholder', 'Efternavn *');
                console.log('Added Efternavn placeholder');
            }
            
            // Translate terms and conditions text
            var registrationForm = document.querySelector('.registration-form');
            if (registrationForm) {
                var allText = registrationForm.innerHTML;
                var originalText = allText;
                
                // Replace in specific order to avoid partial replacements
                allText = allText.replace(/I have read and accepted the terms and conditions/gi, 'Jeg har læst og accepteret vilkår og betingelser');
                allText = allText.replace(/the terms and conditions/gi, 'vilkår og betingelser');
                allText = allText.replace(/terms and conditions/gi, 'vilkår og betingelser');
                allText = allText.replace(/I have read and accepted/gi, 'Jeg har læst og accepteret');
                
                // Clean up any remaining "the" that might be left over
                allText = allText.replace(/Jeg har læst og accepteret the/gi, 'Jeg har læst og accepteret');
                
                if (registrationForm.innerHTML !== allText) {
                    registrationForm.innerHTML = allText;
                    console.log('Translated terms and conditions text');
                }
            }
        }
        
        // Try multiple times to ensure fields are loaded
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', addPlaceholders);
        window.addEventListener('load', addPlaceholders);
        
        // Try again after a short delay in case fields load late
        setTimeout(addPlaceholders, 500);
        </script>

					<script>
				const lazyloadRunObserver = () => {
					const lazyloadBackgrounds = document.querySelectorAll( `.e-con.e-parent:not(.e-lazyloaded)` );
					const lazyloadBackgroundObserver = new IntersectionObserver( ( entries ) => {
						entries.forEach( ( entry ) => {
							if ( entry.isIntersecting ) {
								let lazyloadBackground = entry.target;
								if( lazyloadBackground ) {
									lazyloadBackground.classList.add( 'e-lazyloaded' );
								}
								lazyloadBackgroundObserver.unobserve( entry.target );
							}
						});
					}, { rootMargin: '200px 0px 200px 0px' } );
					lazyloadBackgrounds.forEach( ( lazyloadBackground ) => {
						lazyloadBackgroundObserver.observe( lazyloadBackground );
					} );
				};
				const events = [
					'DOMContentLoaded',
					'elementor/lazyload/observe',
				];
				events.forEach( ( event ) => {
					document.addEventListener( event, lazyloadRunObserver );
				} );
			</script>

				<script type="text/javascript">
		var ajaxurl = "/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php";
		( function() {
			var initialized = [];
			var initialize  = function() {
				var init, id, inPostbox, $wrap;
				var readyState = document.readyState;

				if ( readyState !== 'complete' && readyState !== 'interactive' ) {
					return;
				}

				for ( id in tinyMCEPreInit.mceInit ) {
					if ( initialized.indexOf( id ) > -1 ) {
						continue;
					}

					init      = tinyMCEPreInit.mceInit[id];
					$wrap     = tinymce.$( '#wp-' + id + '-wrap' );
					inPostbox = $wrap.parents( '.postbox' ).length > 0;

					if (
						! init.wp_skip_init &&
						( $wrap.hasClass( 'tmce-active' ) || ! tinyMCEPreInit.qtInit.hasOwnProperty( id ) ) &&
						( readyState === 'complete' || ( ! inPostbox && readyState === 'interactive' ) )
					) {
						tinymce.init( init );
						initialized.push( id );

						if ( ! window.wpActiveEditor ) {
							window.wpActiveEditor = id;
						}
					}
				}
			}

			if ( typeof tinymce !== 'undefined' ) {
				if ( tinymce.Env.ie && tinymce.Env.ie < 11 ) {
					tinymce.$( '.wp-editor-wrap ' ).removeClass( 'tmce-active' ).addClass( 'html-active' );
				} else {
					if ( document.readyState === 'complete' ) {
						initialize();
					} else {
						document.addEventListener( 'readystatechange', initialize );
					}
				}
			}

			if ( typeof quicktags !== 'undefined' ) {
				for ( id in tinyMCEPreInit.qtInit ) {
					quicktags( tinyMCEPreInit.qtInit[id] );

					if ( ! window.wpActiveEditor ) {
						window.wpActiveEditor = id;
					}
				}
			}
		}());
		</script>
			</body>
</html>
